## Diagram 2

```mermaid
graph LR
    ConfigMap[ConfigMap: config-logging]
    ConfigMap --> Metadata
    ConfigMap --> Data
    Metadata --> Name[name: config-logging]
    Metadata --> Namespace[namespace: Release.Namespace]
    Metadata --> Labels[labels: karpenter.labels]
    Metadata --> Annotations[annotations: additionalAnnotations]
    Data --> ZapConfig[zap-logger-config]
    Data --> ControllerLevel[loglevel.controller]
    Data --> WebhookLevel[loglevel.webhook]
    ZapConfig --> Level[level: global]
    ZapConfig --> Sampling[sampling: initial/thereafter]
    ZapConfig --> OutputPaths[outputPaths]
    ZapConfig --> ErrorPaths[errorOutputPaths]
    ZapConfig --> Encoding[encoding: logEncoding]
    ZapConfig --> EncoderConfig[encoderConfig]
```

## Diagram 3

stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> CheckEnabled
    CheckEnabled --> CreateConfigMap: logConfig.enabled = true
    CheckEnabled --> [*]: logConfig.enabled = false
    CreateConfigMap --> SetMetadata
    SetMetadata --> SetData
    SetData --> ApplyConfig
    ApplyConfig --> [*]

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class ConfigMap {
        +string apiVersion
        +string kind
        +Metadata metadata
        +Data data
    }
    class Metadata {
        +string name
        +string namespace
        +map labels
        +map annotations
    }
    class Data {
        +string zapLoggerConfig
        +string loglevelController
        +string loglevelWebhook
    }
    class ZapConfig {
        +string level
        +bool development
        +bool disableStacktrace
        +bool disableCaller
        +Sampling sampling
        +array outputPaths
        +array errorOutputPaths
        +string encoding
        +EncoderConfig encoderConfig
    }
    class Sampling {
        +int initial
        +int thereafter
    }
    class EncoderConfig {
        +string timeKey
        +string levelKey
        +string nameKey
        +string callerKey
        +string messageKey
        +string stacktraceKey
        +string levelEncoder
        +string timeEncoder
    }
    ConfigMap --> Metadata
    ConfigMap --> Data
    Data --> ZapConfig
    ZapConfig --> Sampling
    ZapConfig --> EncoderConfig
```
